msg:As a parent-child hotel, the hotel claimed that the children's playground was not open due to the epidemic, but we looked around and found that there were no children's facilities, and there was only a small room in the lobby showing cartoons.
The hotel environment is still good, there are not many people there just after it opened, and the sanitation and facilities are also very new, which is a bit.
Let‚Äôs focus on services. When booking a room, I redeemed welcome fruit, checked in four hours in advance, room type upgrade, and late check-out. All value-added services were confirmed when the order was confirmed, but they were not enjoyed when checking in. They did not upgrade the room type. When the room was definitely sufficient, they told me that upgrading the room type meant upgrading the floor. Not even early check-in. Instead, they asked us to delay check-in because the room was not cleaned. We waited for two hours before checking in. Welcome fruit. It was delivered the next day after I complained to Ctrip. No one informed me whether late check-out was possible. I called the front desk myself again, and the front desk staff told me that it was OK after I applied. In short, the service is extremely poor and cannot keep up!
The variety of breakfast is average, but the supply of drinks has never kept up. There are only one or two kinds of milk, yogurt, and juice. Guests are always waiting with cups in hand, poor!
In short, I suggest you think twice before placing an order. The so-called international chain five-star hotels will not provide you with corresponding services.
